HTTP Health Check Endpoint Implementations Across Kubernetes, Grafana, and Prometheus\\n\\n## Overview\\nThe three projects use different approaches to implement health check endpoints:\\n\\n## Kubernetes (github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes)\\nKubernetes uses a comprehensive health check framework with three distinct endpoints:\\n\\n### Endpoints\\n- **/healthz**: General health status\\n- **/livez**: Liveness probe (indicates if the server is still running)\\n- **/readyz**: Readiness probe (indicates if the server is ready to accept traffic)\\n\\n### Implementation Architecture\\nThe health check framework is implemented in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/healthz/healthz.go` and integrated through `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/healthz.go`.\\n\\n**Key Components:**\\n1. **HealthChecker Interface** (line 40-44): Defines the contract for health checks with `Name()` and `Check(req *http.Request)` methods\\n\\n2. **Built-in Health Checks** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/healthz/healthz.go):\\n   - **PingHealthz** (line 52): Always returns healthy, serves as a baseline check\\n   - **LogHealthz** (line 67): Monitors logging system health, ensures logs are not blocked\\n   - **InformerSyncHealthz** (NewInformerSyncHealthz, line 105-109): Waits for cache synchronization of informers\\n   - **ShutdownHealthz** (NewShutdownHealthz, line 121-123): Fails when shutdown signal is received\\n   - **Custom Named Checks**: Via `NamedCheck()` and `NamedGroupedCheck()` for domain-specific checks\\n\\n3. **Database Health Checks** - ETcd Integration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/etcd.go, lines 354-413):\\n   - **etcd-health check** (line 359-361): Created via `storagefactory.CreateHealthCheck()`, checks connectivity and health of etcd backend\\n   - **etcd-readiness check** (line 367-369): Created via `storagefactory.CreateReadyCheck()`, ensures etcd is ready to serve requests\\n   - **Multi-server overrides** (lines 371-411): Supports multiple etcd server configurations with separate health checks for each override\\n\\n4. **Handler Installation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/healthz.go, lines 124-140):\\n   - `installHealthz()` installs the /healthz endpoint\\n   - `installReadyz()` installs the /readyz endpoint with a callback for lifecycle signals\\n   - `installLivez()` installs the /livez endpoint\\n   - Each endpoint can have multiple health checks aggregated via `healthCheckRegistry`\\n\\n5. **Grace Periods and Delayed Checks** (healthz.go, lines 142-167):\\n   - Livez checks support grace periods during startup (via `delayedHealthCheck`)\\n   - Readyz has no grace period - must pass before server accepts traffic\\n   - Healthz serves backward compatibility\\n\\n### Configuration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/config.go, lines 197-204)\\nThe server config holds three separate check lists:\\n- `HealthzChecks`: For /healthz endpoint\\n- `LivezChecks`: For /livez endpoint  \\n- `ReadyzChecks`: For /readyz endpoint\\n\\nMethods to add checks:\\n- `AddHealthChecks()` (lines 579-586): Adds to healthz, livez, and readyz\\n- `AddReadyzChecks()` (lines 588-592): Adds only to readyz\\n- `AddLivezChecks()`: Adds only to livez\\n\\n## Prometheus (github.com/prometheus/prometheus)\\nPrometheus uses a simpler, state-based approach:\\n\\n### Endpoints\\n- **/-/healthy**: HTTP health status\\n- **/-/ready**: HTTP readiness status\\n\\n### Implementation (web/web.go)\\n\\n1. **Simple Response Handlers** (lines 591-604):\\n   - `/-/healthy` (line 591-597): Always returns 200 OK with message \\\"{AppName} is Healthy\\\"\\n   - `/-/ready` (line 598-604): Wrapped by `readyf()` middleware that checks internal state\\n   - Both support GET and HEAD methods\\n\\n2. **State-Based Readiness** (lines 658-677):\\n   - `testReady()` function checks `h.ready` atomic value\\n   - Returns 200 OK if state is `Ready`\\n   - Returns 503 Service Unavailable if state is `NotReady` or `Stopping`\\n   - Sets `X-Prometheus-Stopping` header to indicate shutdown state\\n\\n3. **Ready States** (web/web.go):\\n   - `Ready`: Server is operational and ready for requests\\n   - `NotReady`: Server is initializing\\n   - `Stopping`: Server is shutting down\\n\\n4. **No Complex Health Checks**: HTTP Health Check Endpoint Implementations Across Kubernetes, Grafana, and Prometheus\\n\\n## Overview\\nThe three projects use different approaches to implement health check endpoints:\\n\\n## system health, ensures logs are not blocked\\n   - **InformerSyncHealthz** (NewInformerSyncHealthz, line 105-109): Waits for cache synchronization of informers\\n   - **ShutdownHealthz** (NewShutdownHealthz, line 121-123): Fails when shutdown signal is received\\n   - **Custom Named Checks**: Via `NamedCheck()` and `NamedGroupedCheck()` for domain-specific checks\\n\\n3. **Database ready to serve requests\\n   - **Multi-server overrides** (lines 371-411): Supports multiple etcd server configurations with separate health checks for each override\\n\\n4. **Handler Installation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/healthz.go, lines 124-140):\\n   - `installHealthz()` installs the /healthz endpoint\\n   - `installReadyz()` installs the /readyz endpoint with a callback for lifecycle signals\\n   - `installLivez()` installs the /livez endpoint\\n   - Each endpoint can have multiple health checks aggregated via `healthCheckRegistry`\\n\\n5. **Grace Periods and Delayed Checks** (healthz.go, lines 142-167):\\n   - Livez checks support grace periods during startup (via `delayedHealthCheck`)\\n   - Readyz has no grace period - must pass before server accepts traffic\\n   - Healthz serves backward compatibility\\n\\n### Configuration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/config.go, lines 197-204)\\nThe server config holds three separate check lists:\\n- Handlers** (lines 591-604):\\n   - `/-/healthy` (line 591-597): Always returns 200 OK with message \\\"{AppName} is Healthy\\\"\\n   - `/-/ready` (line 598-604): Wrapped by `readyf()` middleware that (web/web.go):\\n   - `Ready`: Server is operational and ready for requests\\n   - `NotReady`: Server is initializing\\n   - `Stopping`: Server is shutting down\\n\\n4. **No Complex Health Checks**:
